    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[PersonId], [p].[Id], [p].[Name], [p].[PersonType], [p].[PersonalCodeOrRegistrationNumber]
    FROM [People] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[PersonId] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [l].[LandPropertyId], [l].[CadastralMark], [l].[Name], [l].[PersonId], [l].[Status], [t1].[PlotId], [t1].[CadastralMark] AS [CadastralMark0], [t1].[DateOfSurvey], [t1].[LandPropertyId] AS [LandPropertyId0], [t1].[TotalAreaInHectares], [t1].[LandTypeId], [t1].[AreaInHectares], [t1].[PlotId0], [t1].[Type]
    FROM [LandProperties] AS [l]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [p0].[PlotId], [p0].[CadastralMark], [p0].[DateOfSurvey], [p0].[LandPropertyId], [p0].[TotalAreaInHectares], [l0].[LandTypeId], [l0].[AreaInHectares], [l0].[PlotId] AS [PlotId0], [l0].[Type]
        FROM [Plots] AS [p0]
        LEFT JOIN [LandTypes] AS [l0] ON [p0].[PlotId] = [l0].[PlotId]
    ) AS [t1] ON [l].[LandPropertyId] = [t1].[LandPropertyId]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[PersonId] = [t0].[PersonId]
ORDER BY [t].[PersonId], [t0].[LandPropertyId], [t0].[PlotId]
